<li>Sapmi Park – Located Karasjok, Norway, Sapmi Park<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup> and visitor center presents the Sami culture and its history through exhibits and a special effect theater presentation, entitled "The Magic Theater"<sup id="cite_ref-Sapmi_Magic_Theater_170-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sapmi_Magic_Theater-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup> designed originally by award-winning experience designer <a href="/wiki/Bob_Rogers_(designer)" title="Bob Rogers (designer)">Bob Rogers (designer)</a> and the design team BRC Imagination Arts.<sup id="cite_ref-Sapmi_Magic_Theater_170-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sapmi_Magic_Theater-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sami_films">Sami films</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=S%C3%A1mi_people&amp;action=edit&amp;section=77" title="Edit section: Sami films">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Pathfinder_(1987_film)" title="Pathfinder (1987 film)">Pathfinder</a></i> (<i>Ofelaš</i>), 1988 film nominated for the Academy Award for Best Foreign Film; filmed in Norway featuring Sami actors speaking in Sami</li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Cuckoo_(film)" title="The Cuckoo (film)">The Cuckoo</a></i> (<i>Kukushka</i>) (2002), film set during World War II with a Sami woman as one of the main characters</li>
<li><i>Frozen 2</i> (2019), will feature Sami characters old and new; there will be a Sami language dubbing of the film<sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Give_Us_Our_Skeletons" title="Give Us Our Skeletons">Give Us Our Skeletons</a></i>, a 1999 documentary about the scientific racism and racial classification movement carried out on the Sami</li>
<li><i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Herdswoman_(film)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Herdswoman (film) (page does not exist)">Herdswoman</a></i> (2008), a documentary about land rights disputes in reindeer grazing areas</li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Kautokeino_Rebellion" title="The Kautokeino Rebellion">The Kautokeino Rebellion</a></i> (2008), feature film that concerns the ethnic-religious Sami revolt in Guovdageaidnu of 1852</li>
<li><i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Last_Yoik_in_Saami_Forests%3F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Last Yoik in Saami Forests? (page does not exist)">Last Yoik in Saami Forests?</a></i> (2007), made for the United Nations, a documentary about land rights disputes in Finnish Lapland</li>
<li><i>Magic Mushrooms and Reindeer: Weird Nature</i>, short video on the use of <i><a href="/wiki/Amanita_muscaria" title="Amanita muscaria">Amanita muscaria</a></i> mushrooms by the Sami people and their <a href="/wiki/Reindeer" title="Reindeer">reindeer</a>, produced by the <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a><sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i>Midnight Sun</i> (2016), crime series which revolves around Sami culture and conflicts of Sami culture with modern Swedish society</li>
<li><i>The Sami</i>, a Mushkeg Media documentary about the state of aboriginal languages</li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Sami_Blood" title="Sami Blood">Sami Blood</a></i> (2016), a movie chronicling the life of a Sami girl taken into a Swedish boarding school to be assimilated as a Swede<sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Suddenly_Sami&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Suddenly Sami (page does not exist)">Suddenly Sami</a></i> (2009), in which the filmmaker finds out that her mother has been hiding her Arctic indigenous Sámi heritage from her</li>
<li><i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wolf_(2008_film)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Wolf (2008 film) (page does not exist)">Wolf</a></i>, an examination of how the traditions of the Sami villagers in northern Sweden are confronted with modern-day society</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sami_books">Sami books</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=S%C3%A1mi_people&amp;action=edit&amp;section=81" title="Edit section: Sami books">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>The <i><a href="/wiki/Germania_(book)" title="Germania (book)">Germania</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Tacitus" title="Tacitus">Tacitus</a> (the chapter on <a href="/wiki/Fenni" title="Fenni">Fenni</a>)</li>
<li><i>Vigilant Ancestor: A World of Secrets Whispered in My Ear</i>, by H. D. Rennerfeldt. <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/><a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-1-62675-021-0" title="Special:BookSources/978-1-62675-021-0">978-1-62675-021-0</a>.</li>
<li><i>The Sami Peoples of the North: A Social and Cultural History</i>, by Neil Kent. <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/><a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-1-84904-257-4" title="Special:BookSources/978-1-84904-257-4">978-1-84904-257-4</a>.</li>

Van Cleef. <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/><a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-1-4382-2189-2" title="Special:BookSources/978-1-4382-2189-2">978-1-4382-2189-2</a>.</li></ul>
